 This time Devauthani Ekadashi is on 8 November
 devuthni ekadshi ko hariprabodhini ekadshi or devotthana ekadshi bhi kehete hai
 It is believed that Lord Vishnu sleeps for four months on Ashadh Shukla Ekadashi and wakes up on Kartik Shukla Ekadashi
 devuthni ekadshi ke din chaturmaas kaa ant ho jaataa he

 jab dev (bhagwaan vishnu ) jaagate hai, tabhi koi mangalik kaary sampann ho paata he

 is din upwas rakhane kaa vishesh mahatv he
 It is said that this leads to salvation
 devuthni ekadshi ke din vrath rakhane ke niyam- nirjal yaa keval jaleey padaarthon par upwas rakhana chahie
 - If the patient is old, child, or busy person, then only a bella should be fasted
 - bhagwaan vishnu yaa apane isht-dev kii upasna karen
 - Do not eat tamasic food (onion, garlic, meat, liqueur, stale food) at all
 - aaj ke din " namo bhagavate vasudevy namah " mantra kaa jaap karnaa chahie
 - If your moon is weak or has mental problem, then keep a fast of water and fruits or waterless Ekadashi
 kya he devuthni ekadshi kii puja vidhi?- ganne kaa mandap banaaen, bich main chowk banaaya jaataa he
 If you want, you can place a picture or statue of Lord Vishnu in the center of the square
 - chowk ke saath hi bhagwaan ke charan chinh banaaye jate hai ,jisko ki dhank diya jaataa he

 - The feet of the Lord are duly worshiped at dawn and the feet are awakened by touching them
 - shankh-ghanta-or kirthan kii dhwani kii jaati he

 - iske baad se saare mangal kaary vidhivat shuru kiye ja sakate hai
 - What is said by touching the feet of God is fulfilled
